\subsection{详细描述}
Macros for handling GL dispatch tables.

For each known GL function, there are 3 macros in this file. The first macro is named C\+A\+L\+L\+\_\+\+Func\+Name and is used to call that GL function using the specified dispatch table. The other 2 macros, called G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+Func\+Name can S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+Func\+Name, are used to get and set the dispatch pointer for the named function in the specified dispatch table.

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{S\+E\+T\+\_\+by\+\_\+offset}{SET\_by\_offset}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#\hyperlink{structdefine}{define} S\+E\+T\+\_\+by\+\_\+offset(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{disp,  }\item[{}]{offset,  }\item[{}]{fn }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries 值\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
\textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{ \(\backslash\)
        if ( (offset) < 0 ) \{ \(\backslash\)
            \textcolor{comment}{/* fprintf( stderr, "[%s:%u] SET\_by\_offset(%p, %d, %s)!\(\backslash\)n", */} \(\backslash\)
            \textcolor{comment}{/*         \_\_func\_\_, \_\_LINE\_\_, disp, offset, # fn); */} \(\backslash\)
            \textcolor{comment}{/* abort(); */} \(\backslash\)
        \} \(\backslash\)
        else \{ \(\backslash\)
            ( (\_glapi\_proc *) (disp) )[offset] = (\_glapi\_proc) fn; \(\backslash\)
        \} \(\backslash\)
    \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(0)
\end{DoxyCode}
